--
-- EXP_FULL_DATABASE  (Role) 
--
CREATE ROLE EXP_FULL_DATABASE NOT IDENTIFIED;

GRANT READ ANY FILE GROUP TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT EXECUTE ANY PROCEDURE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT RESUMABLE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT SELECT ANY TABLE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT EXECUTE ANY TYPE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT EXEMPT REDACTION POLICY TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT BACKUP ANY TABLE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT ADMINISTER SQL MANAGEMENT OBJECT TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT CREATE SESSION TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
BEGIN
SYS.DBMS_RESOURCE_MANAGER_PRIVS.GRANT_SYSTEM_PRIVILEGE
  (GRANTEE_NAME   => 'EXP_FULL_DATABASE', 
   PRIVILEGE_NAME => 'ADMINISTER_RESOURCE_MANAGER',
   ADMIN_OPTION   => FALSE);
END;
/
GRANT SELECT ANY SEQUENCE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;
GRANT CREATE TABLE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;

GRANT EXECUTE_CATALOG_ROLE TO EXP_FULL_DATABASE;

--
-- CS_CHUKYSO  (Table) 
--
CREATE TABLE MPLIS.CS_CHUKYSO
(
  CHUKYSOID         VARCHAR2(36 BYTE)           DEFAULT SYS_GUID()            NOT NULL,
  NHACUNGCAPID      VARCHAR2(36 BYTE)           NOT NULL,
  TOCHUCID          VARCHAR2(36 BYTE)           NOT NULL,
  NGUOIDUNGID       VARCHAR2(36 BYTE)           NOT NULL,
  LOAICHUKYSO       NUMBER,
  NGUOIDUNGTEN      VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  TENTOCHUC         VARCHAR2(150 BYTE),
  CHUCVU            VARCHAR2(50 BYTE),
  NOICONGTAC        VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  NGAYCOHIEULUC     DATE,
  NGAYHETHIEULUC    DATE,
  TRANGTHAIXACTHUC  NUMBER(1),
  "uId"             VARCHAR2(36 BYTE),
  THOIDIEMKHOITAO   DATE,
  THOIDIEMCAPNHAT   DATE,
  NGUOICAPNHATID    VARCHAR2(36 BYTE),
  CA                LONG
)
TABLESPACE MPLIS
RESULT_CACHE (MODE DEFAULT)
PCTUSED    0
PCTFREE    10
INITRANS   1
MAXTRANS   255
STORAGE    (
            INITIAL          128K
            NEXT             1M
            MINEXTENTS       1
            MAXEXTENTS       UNLIMITED
            PCTINCREASE      0
            BUFFER_POOL      DEFAULT
            FLASH_CACHE      DEFAULT
            CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT
           )
NOCOMPRESS ;

COMMENT ON TABLE MPLIS.CS_CHUKYSO IS 'Ch¿u trách nhi¿m thi¿t k¿: KS. Tr¿n Duy H¿nh - C¿c Ðang ký d¿t dai';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MPLIS.CS_CHUKYSO.LOAICHUKYSO IS '1: T¿ ch¿c
0: Cá nhân';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MPLIS.CS_CHUKYSO.TRANGTHAIXACTHUC IS '1: Ðã xác th¿c
0: Chua xác th¿c';

--
-- FN_LAYDUONGDANFILEHSQ  (Function) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION MPLIS.FN_LAYDUONGDANFILEHSQ 
(
  d_XAID IN VARCHAR2  
 , d_HOSOID IN VARCHAR2  
) RETURN VARCHAR2
AS 
 d_duongDan varchar(250);
 d_maXa varchar2(36);
 d_maHuyen varchar2(36);
 d_maTinh varchar2(36);
 d_huyenId varchar2(36);
 d_tinhId varchar2(36);
 
BEGIN
-- select ---------------;
 SELECT MAXA into d_maXa from HC_XA where HC_XA.XAID = d_XAID;
 SELECT HUYENID into d_huyenId from HC_XA where HC_XA.XAID = d_XAID;
 SELECT MAHUYEN into d_maHuyen from HC_HUYEN where HC_HUYEN.HUYENID = d_huyenId;
 SELECT TINHID into d_tinhId from HC_HUYEN where HC_HUYEN.HUYENID = d_huyenId;
 SELECT MATINH into d_maTinh from HC_TINH where HC_TINH.TINHID = d_tinhId;


RETURN 'T' || d_maTinh || '/' || 'H' || d_maHuyen || '/' || 'X' || d_maXa || '/' || 'HS' ||  d_HOSOID;
--L¿Y ÐU¿NG D¿N LUU FILE ;

END FN_LAYDUONGDANFILEHSQ;
/

--
-- VIEW_NGUOIDUNG_HTXA  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_NGUOIDUNG_HTXA
(XAID, NGUOIDUNGID, HOTENNGUOIDUNG, TENDANGNHAP, CAPNGUOIDUNG, 
 TENXA)
AS 
SELECT X.XAID,X.NGUOIDUNGID,N.HOTENNGUOIDUNG,N.TENDANGNHAP,N.CAPNGUOIDUNG
, XA.TENXA

FROM 

HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG  X
LEFT JOIN HT_NGUOIDUNG N ON N.NGUOIDUNGID = X.NGUOIDUNGID
LEFT JOIN HC_XA XA ON XA.XAID = X.XAID;


--
-- VIEW_QT_TTHC  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_QT_TTHC
(THUTUCHANHCHINHID, BOTHUTUCHANHCHINHID, TENTHUTUCHANHCHINH, CAP, DONVIHANHCHINHID, 
 THOIHANGIAIQUYETTOIDA, LEPHI, THUTU, TENTINH, TINHID, 
 TENHUYEN, HUYENID, TINHIDBYHUYEN, HUYENIDBYXA, TENXA, 
 XAID, TENBOTHUTUCHANHCHINH)
AS 
SELECT TTHC.THUTUCHANHCHINHID,
  TTHC.BOTHUTUCHANHCHINHID,
  TTHC.TENTHUTUCHANHCHINH,
  TTHC.CAP,
  TTHC.DONVIHANHCHINHID,
  TTHC.THOIHANGIAIQUYETTOIDA,
  TTHC.LEPHI,
  SUBSTR(TTHC.TENTHUTUCHANHCHINH,0,2) AS  THUTU,
  T.TENTINH,
  T.TINHID,
  H.TENHUYEN,
  H.HUYENID, 
  (H.TINHID) TINHIDBYHUYEN, 
  (X.HUYENID) HUYENIDBYXA,
  X.TENXA,
  X.XAID,
  D.TENBOTHUTUCHANHCHINH
FROM QT_THUTUCHANHCHINH TTHC
left join HC_TINH T on T.TINHID= TTHC.DONVIHANHCHINHID
left join HC_HUYEN H on H.HUYENID= TTHC.DONVIHANHCHINHID
left join HC_XA X on X.XAID= TTHC.DONVIHANHCHINHID
left join DM_BOTHUTUCHANHCHINH D on D.BOTHUTUCHANHCHINHID = TTHC.BOTHUTUCHANHCHINHID
ORDER BY THUTU ASC;


--
-- HTV_MAUGIAYTO  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HTV_MAUGIAYTO
(MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHSID, CAP, MADONVIHANHCHINHID, TEMPLATE, GIAYTOKEMTHEOHSID, 
 KYHIEU, TENGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS, MAUGIAYTO, THUTUSAPXEP, TENTINH, 
 MATINH, TINHID, MAHUYEN, TENHUYEN, HUYENID, 
 MAXA, TENXA, TENDONVIHANHCHINH)
AS 
SELECT HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHSID,HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.CAP,HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.MADONVIHANHCHINHID,HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.TEMPLATE, DM_GIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.GIAYTOKEMTHEOHSID, DM_GIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.KYHIEU, DM_GIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.TENGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS, DM_GIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.MAUGIAYTO, DM_GIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.THUTUSAPXEP,HC_TINH.TENTINH,HC_TINH.MATINH,HC_HUYEN.TINHID,HC_HUYEN.MAHUYEN,HC_HUYEN.TENHUYEN,HC_XA.HUYENID,HC_XA.MAXA,HC_XA.TENXA,HC_TINH.TENTINH || HC_HUYEN.TENHUYEN || HC_XA.TENXA AS TENDONVIHANHCHINH
    
FROM HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS INNER JOIN DM_GIAYTOKEMTHEOHS ON HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.GIAYTOKEMTHEOHSID = DM_GIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.GIAYTOKEMTHEOHSID LEFT JOIN HC_TINH ON HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.MADONVIHANHCHINHID = HC_TINH.TINHID LEFT JOIN HC_HUYEN ON HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.MADONVIHANHCHINHID = HC_HUYEN.HUYENID LEFT JOIN HC_XA ON HT_MAUGIAYTOKEMTHEOHS.MADONVIHANHCHINHID = HC_XA.XAID;


--
-- VIEW_NGUONGOCTHUA  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_NGUONGOCTHUA
(THUADATID, LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID, MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID, MANGUONGOCSUDUNG, TENNGUONGOCSUDUNG)
AS 
SELECT  M.THUADATID, DMNG.LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID,M.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID,
 DMNG.MANGUONGOCSUDUNG,DMNG.TENNGUONGOCSUDUNG             
                FROM DC_MUCDICHSUDUNGDAT M
                LEFT JOIN DC_NGUONGOCSUDUNG NG ON M.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID = NG.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID
                LEFT JOIN DM_LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNG DMNG ON NG.LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID = DMNG.LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID 
              
ORDER BY THUADATID;


--
-- VIEWNG_NHOM  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEWNG_NHOM
(NGUOIID, LOAIDOITUONGID, NHOMNGUOIID, THANHPHANID, LOAIDOITUONG)
AS 
select ng.NGUOIID,ng.LOAIDOITUONGID,NhomN.NHOMNGUOIID,tvnh.THANHPHANID,
  tvnh.LOAIDOITUONG
from DC_NGUOI ng
 left join DC_NHOMNGUOI NhomN on ng.chitietID =NhomN.NHOMNGUOIID
 left join DC_NHOMNGUOI_THANHVIEN tvnh on NhomN.NHOMNGUOIID =tvnh.NHOMNGUOIID
 where ng.loaidoituongid =6
 order by NhomN.NHOMNGUOIID;


--
-- VIEWNG_HOGIADINH  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEWNG_HOGIADINH
(NGUOIID, CHITIETID, CHUHO, CANHANID, LOAIDOITUONGID, 
 HOTEN, GIOITINH, SOGIAYTO, TENQUOCGIATV, MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN)
AS 
SELECT B.NGUOIID,B.CHITIETID,B.CHUHO,A.CANHANID, B.LOAIDOITUONGID,
A.HOTEN,A.GIOITINH, A.SOGIAYTO,
A.TENQUOCGIATV,A.MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN
FROM
(SELECT  CN.HOTEN,CN.GIOITINH, CN.CANHANID, GT.SOGIAYTO,QT.TENQUOCGIATV, DMGT.MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN
				FROM DC_CANHAN CN
                LEFT JOIN  DC_GIAYTOTUYTHAN GT ON GT.CANHANID = CN.CANHANID
				LEFT JOIN  DM_QUOCTICH QT ON QT.QUOCTICHID =CN.QUOCTICHID
                LEFT JOIN  DM_LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN DMGT ON DMGT.LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHANID = GT.LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHANID
                ) A
		INNER JOIN
(SELECT NG.NGUOIID ,NG.LOAIDOITUONGID,
		NG.CHITIETID, HGD.CHUHO,  HGD.VOCHONG ,
 		TVH.CANHANID AS THANHVIENHO,
 		HGD.DIACHI AS DIACHIHOGD
FROM DC_NGUOI NG
 		LEFT JOIN DC_HOGIADINH HGD ON NG.CHITIETID =HGD.HOGIADINHID
 		LEFT JOIN DC_HOGIADINH_THANHVIEN TVH ON HGD.HOGIADINHID =TVH.HOGIADINHID
               ) B
 ON A.CANHANID = B.CHUHO
  OR A.CANHANID = B.VOCHONG
  OR A.CANHANID = B.THANHVIENHO
ORDER BY B.NGUOIID ,B.CHITIETID;


--
-- VIEWNG_CANHAN  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEWNG_CANHAN
(NGUOIID, LOAIDOITUONGID, CHITIETID, HOTEN, GIOITINH, 
 SOGIAYTO, TENQUOCGIATV, MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN, DIACHIDAYDU)
AS 
SELECT B.NGUOIID,B.LOAIDOITUONGID,B.CHITIETID,
A.HOTEN,A.GIOITINH, A.SOGIAYTO,
A.TENQUOCGIATV,A.MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN,A.DIACHIDAYDU
FROM
(SELECT  CN.HOTEN,CN.DIACHIDAYDU,CN.GIOITINH, CN.CANHANID, GT.SOGIAYTO,QT.TENQUOCGIATV, DMGT.MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN
				FROM DC_CANHAN CN
                LEFT JOIN  DC_GIAYTOTUYTHAN GT ON GT.CANHANID = CN.CANHANID
				LEFT JOIN  DM_QUOCTICH QT ON QT.QUOCTICHID =CN.QUOCTICHID
                LEFT JOIN  DM_LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN DMGT ON DMGT.LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHANID = GT.LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHANID
                ) A
		INNER JOIN
(SELECT N.NGUOIID,N.CHITIETID,
  N.LOAIDOITUONGID
				FROM DC_NGUOI N
                WHERE N.LOAIDOITUONGID =1
               ) B
ON A.CANHANID =B.CHITIETID
ORDER BY B.NGUOIID;


--
-- VIEWNG_VOCHONG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEWNG_VOCHONG
(NGUOIID, CHITIETID, CHONG, VO, LOAIDOITUONGID, 
 HOTEN, GIOITINH, SOGIAYTO, TENQUOCGIATV, MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN, 
 DIACHIDAYDU)
AS 
SELECT B.NGUOIID,B.CHITIETID,B.CHONG, B.VO,B.LOAIDOITUONGID,
A.HOTEN,A.GIOITINH, A.SOGIAYTO,
A.TENQUOCGIATV,A.MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN,A.DIACHIDAYDU
FROM
(SELECT  CN.HOTEN,CN.DIACHIDAYDU,CN.GIOITINH, CN.CANHANID, GT.SOGIAYTO,QT.TENQUOCGIATV, DMGT.MALOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN
				FROM DC_CANHAN CN
                LEFT JOIN  DC_GIAYTOTUYTHAN GT ON GT.CANHANID = CN.CANHANID
				LEFT JOIN  DM_QUOCTICH QT ON QT.QUOCTICHID =CN.QUOCTICHID
                LEFT JOIN  DM_LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHAN DMGT ON DMGT.LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHANID = GT.LOAIGIAYTOTUYTHANID
                ) A
		INNER JOIN
(SELECT N.NGUOIID,VC.CHONG, VC.VO,N.CHITIETID,
  N.LOAIDOITUONGID
				FROM DC_NGUOI N
                INNER JOIN  DC_VOCHONG VC ON VC.VOCHONGID =N.CHITIETID
                WHERE N.LOAIDOITUONGID =2
               ) B
ON A.CANHANID =B.VO OR A.CANHANID =B.CHONG
ORDER BY B.NGUOIID;


--
-- VIEWNG_TOCHUC_CONGDONG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEWNG_TOCHUC_CONGDONG
(NGUOIID, CHITIETID, LOAIDOITUONGID, TENCONGDONG, NGUOIDAIDIENCONGDONGID, 
 DIADANHCUTRU, TENTOCHUC, NGUOIDAIDIENTOCHUCID, SOQUYETDINH, NGAYQUYETDINH, 
 LOAIQUYETDINHTHANHLAP, MADOANHNGHIEP, MASOTHUE, LOAITOCHUC, DIACHI)
AS 
SELECT NG.NGUOIID,NG.CHITIETID,NG.LOAIDOITUONGID,
 CDG.TENCONGDONG,
 CDG.NGUOIDAIDIEN AS NGUOIDAIDIENCONGDONGID,
 CDG.DIADANHCUTRU,
  TC.TENTOCHUC,
  TC.NGUOIDAIDIENID AS NGUOIDAIDIENTOCHUCID,
  TC.SOQUYETDINH,
  TC.NGAYQUYETDINH,
  TC.LOAIQUYETDINHTHANHLAP,
  TC.MADOANHNGHIEP,
  TC.MASOTHUE,
  TC.LOAITOCHUC,
  TC.DIACHI
FROM DC_NGUOI NG
 LEFT JOIN DC_CONGDONG CDG ON NG.CHITIETID =CDG.CONGDONGID
 LEFT JOIN DC_TOCHUC TC ON NG.CHITIETID =TC.TOCHUCID
 WHERE NG.LOAIDOITUONGID = 5 OR NG.LOAIDOITUONGID = 4;


--
-- HSV_DVHC_NGUOIDUNG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HSV_DVHC_NGUOIDUNG
(HOSOID, LAHOSOHIENTAI, XAID, NGUOIDUNGID, HUYENID, 
 TINHID, MAHOSO, MAHOSO_TAM, MAHOSO_ST, MAHOSO_MB, 
 MAHOSO_TB, TENHOSO, SOTODAIDIEN, SOTHUADAIDIEN, NGAYHOSO, 
 PHONG, KE, NGAN, HOP, TENHOP, 
 DALIENKETCSDL_KG, DALIENKETCSDL_TT, GHICHU, TENXA, TENHUYEN, 
 TENTINH, VTPHONG, VTNKE, VTNNGAN, VTHOP, 
 VTTENHOP)
AS 
SELECT HS_HOSO.HOSOID,HS_HOSO.LAHOSOHIENTAI,HC_XA.XAID ,HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID, HC_HUYEN.HUYENID,HC_TINH.TINHID
,HS_HOSO.MAHOSO,HS_HOSO.MAHOSO_TAM,HS_HOSO.MAHOSO_ST,HS_HOSO.MAHOSO_MB, HS_HOSO.MAHOSO_TB
,HS_HOSO.TENHOSO,HS_HOSO.SOTODAIDIEN,HS_HOSO.SOTHUADAIDIEN
,HS_HOSO.NGAYHOSO,HS_HOSO.PHONG,HS_HOSO.KE,HS_HOSO.NGAN
,HS_HOSO.HOP,HS_HOSO.TENHOP,HS_HOSO.DALIENKETCSDL_KG,HS_HOSO.DALIENKETCSDL_TT,HS_HOSO.GHICHU
,HC_XA.TENXA,HC_HUYEN.TENHUYEN,HC_TINH.TENTINH

,(SELECT TENVITRILUUTRU FROM HS_VITRILUUTRU WHERE HS_VITRILUUTRU.VITRILUUTRUID = HS_HOSO.PHONG) VTPHONG
,(SELECT TENVITRILUUTRU FROM HS_VITRILUUTRU WHERE HS_VITRILUUTRU.VITRILUUTRUID = HS_HOSO.KE) VTNKE
,(SELECT TENVITRILUUTRU FROM HS_VITRILUUTRU WHERE HS_VITRILUUTRU.VITRILUUTRUID = HS_HOSO.NGAN) VTNNGAN
,(SELECT TENVITRILUUTRU FROM HS_VITRILUUTRU WHERE HS_VITRILUUTRU.VITRILUUTRUID = HS_HOSO.HOP) VTHOP
,(SELECT MOTA FROM HS_VITRILUUTRU WHERE HS_VITRILUUTRU.VITRILUUTRUID = HS_HOSO.HOP) VTTENHOP

FROM HS_HOSO LEFT JOIN HC_XA ON HC_XA.XAID = HS_HOSO.XAID 
LEFT JOIN HC_HUYEN ON HC_HUYEN.HUYENID = HC_XA.HUYENID
LEFT JOIN HC_TINH ON HC_TINH.TINHID = HC_HUYEN.TINHID
LEFT JOIN HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.XAID = HS_HOSO.XAID 
LEFT JOIN HT_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID = HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID;


--
-- HSV_XA_NGUOIDUNG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HSV_XA_NGUOIDUNG
(NGUOIDUNGID, XAID, HUYENID, TENXA)
AS 
SELECT DISTINCT HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID,HC_XA.XAID,HC_XA.HUYENID,HC_XA.TENXA
    
FROM HT_NGUOIDUNG INNER JOIN HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID = HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID INNER JOIN HC_XA ON HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.XAID = HC_XA.XAID;


--
-- HSV_HUYEN_NGUOIDUNG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HSV_HUYEN_NGUOIDUNG
(NGUOIDUNGID, HUYENID, TINHID, TENHUYEN)
AS 
SELECT DISTINCT HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID,HC_HUYEN.HUYENID,HC_HUYEN.TINHID,HC_HUYEN.TENHUYEN
    
FROM HT_NGUOIDUNG INNER JOIN HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID = HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID INNER JOIN HC_XA ON HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.XAID = HC_XA.XAID INNER JOIN HC_HUYEN ON HC_XA.HUYENID = HC_HUYEN.HUYENID;


--
-- HSV_TINH_NGUOIDUNG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HSV_TINH_NGUOIDUNG
(NGUOIDUNGID, TINHID, TENTINH, MATINH)
AS 
SELECT DISTINCT HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID,HC_TINH.TINHID,HC_TINH.TENTINH,HC_TINH.MATINH
    
FROM HT_NGUOIDUNG INNER JOIN HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID = HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID INNER JOIN HC_XA ON HT_XA_NGUOIDUNG.XAID = HC_XA.XAID INNER JOIN HC_HUYEN ON HC_XA.HUYENID = HC_HUYEN.HUYENID INNER JOIN HC_TINH ON HC_HUYEN.TINHID = HC_TINH.TINHID;


--
-- HSV_THONGKEHOSO  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HSV_THONGKEHOSO
(XAID, HUYENID, TINHID, TENXA, TENHUYEN, 
 TENTINH, SOLUONGHOSO, SOLUONGFILE, TONGKICHTHUOC)
AS 
SELECT HC_XA.XAID,HC_HUYEN.HUYENID,HC_TINH.TINHID, HC_XA.TENXA,HC_HUYEN.TENHUYEN,HC_TINH.TENTINH,COUNT(DISTINCT HS_HOSO.HOSOID) AS "SOLUONGHOSO",COUNT(HS_THANHPHANHOSO.THANHPHANHOSOID) AS "SOLUONGFILE",ROUND(SUM(HS_THANHPHANHOSO.KICHTHUOC)/1048576,2) AS "TONGKICHTHUOC"

FROM HS_THANHPHANHOSO RIGHT JOIN HS_HOSO ON HS_THANHPHANHOSO.HOSOID = HS_HOSO.HOSOID INNER JOIN HC_XA ON HC_XA.XAID = HS_HOSO.XAID 
INNER JOIN HC_HUYEN ON HC_HUYEN.HUYENID = HC_XA.HUYENID
INNER JOIN HC_TINH ON HC_TINH.TINHID = HC_HUYEN.TINHID

GROUP BY HC_TINH.TINHID,HC_TINH.TENTINH,HC_HUYEN.HUYENID,HC_HUYEN.TENHUYEN,HC_XA.XAID,HC_XA.TENXA;


--
-- HTV_NGUOIDUNG_UNGDUNG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HTV_NGUOIDUNG_UNGDUNG
(NGUOIDUNGID, LOAINGUOIDUNG, UNGDUNGID, TENUNGDUNG, CHOPHEPSUDUNG, 
 THUTUSAPXEP, URL, MAUNGDUNG)
AS 
SELECT DISTINCT HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID,HT_NGUOIDUNG.LOAINGUOIDUNG,HT_UNGDUNG.UNGDUNGID,HT_UNGDUNG.TENUNGDUNG,HT_UNGDUNG.CHOPHEPSUDUNG,HT_UNGDUNG.THUTUSAPXEP,HT_UNGDUNG.URL,HT_UNGDUNG.MAUNGDUNG
    
FROM HT_NGUOIDUNG INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID = HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID  INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC ON HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG.TOCHUCID = HT_TOCHUC.TOCHUCID INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG ON HT_TOCHUC.TOCHUCID = HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG.TOCHUCID INNER JOIN HT_NHOMCHUCNANG ON HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID = HT_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID INNER JOIN HT_UNGDUNG ON HT_NHOMCHUCNANG.UNGDUNGID = HT_UNGDUNG.UNGDUNGID;


--
-- HTV_NGUOIDUNG_MENU  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HTV_NGUOIDUNG_MENU
(NGUOIDUNGID, LOAINGUOIDUNG, MENUID, KHOACHAID, URL, 
 TENMENU, CHOPHEPSUDUNG, THUTUSAPXEP, TENUNGDUNG, MAUNGDUNG, 
 THUTUSAPXEPMENU)
AS 
SELECT HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID, HT_NGUOIDUNG.LOAINGUOIDUNG, HT_MENU.MENUID,HT_MENU.KHOACHAID,HT_MENU.URL,HT_MENU.TENMENU,HT_MENU.CHOPHEPSUDUNG,HT_UNGDUNG.THUTUSAPXEP,HT_UNGDUNG.TENUNGDUNG,HT_UNGDUNG.MAUNGDUNG,HT_MENU.THUTUSAPXEP AS "THUTUSAPXEPMENU"
    
FROM HT_NGUOIDUNG INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID = HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID  INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC ON HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG.TOCHUCID = HT_TOCHUC.TOCHUCID INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG ON HT_TOCHUC.TOCHUCID = HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG.TOCHUCID INNER JOIN HT_NHOMCHUCNANG ON HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID = HT_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID INNER JOIN HT_NHOMCHUCNANG_MENU ON HT_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID = HT_NHOMCHUCNANG_MENU.NHOMCHUCNANGID INNER JOIN HT_MENU ON HT_NHOMCHUCNANG_MENU.MENUID = HT_MENU.MENUID INNER JOIN HT_UNGDUNG ON HT_MENU.UNGDUNGID = HT_UNGDUNG.UNGDUNGID;


--
-- QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN_IN_UP  (Trigger) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER MPLIS.QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN_IN_UP
  before update or insert  ON MPLIS.QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN  
  for each row
declare
  v_date date := sysdate;
begin
  --neu la insert 
  if inserting then
    :new.THOIDIEMKHOITAO := v_date;
    :new.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT := v_date;
  end if;
  --neu la update
  if updating then
    :new.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT := v_date;
  end if;

end;
/

  before update or insert  ON MPLIS.DC_HOGIADINH_THANHVIEN  
  for each row

  --neu la insert 
  if inserting then
    :new.THOIDIEMKHOITAO := v_date;

  end if;

end;

/

--
-- QUYTRINH_HOSO  (Package Body) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE PACKAGE BODY MPLIS.QUYTRINH_HOSO AS
    
    PROCEDURE LuuXuLyHoSo_TamThoi(hstn_id IN STRING, sodoqt_id IN STRING);
    PROCEDURE LuuTrangThaiHoSo_TamThoi(hstiepnhan_id IN STRING, sodoqt_id IN STRING, xulyhs_id IN STRING);
    PROCEDURE LuuFileDinhKemHoSo_TamThoi (hstiepnhan_id IN STRING);
            
    PROCEDURE LuuHoSoTiepNhan_TamThoi(hstn_id IN STRING, sodoquytrinh_id IN STRING, stlydoxoatamthoi IN STRING) AS
  
          --PROCEDURE LuuXuLyHoSo_TamThoi(hstn_id IN STRING, sodoqt_id IN STRING);
          
          CANBOTIEPNHANIDfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.CANBOTIEPNHANID%type;
          CAPfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.CAP%type;
          DIACHINGUOINHANKETQUAfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.DIACHINGUOINHANKETQUA%type; 
          DIACHINGUOINOPHSfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.DIACHINGUOINOPHS%type;
          DONVIHANHCHINHIDfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.DONVIHANHCHINHID%type;
          EMAILfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.EMAIL%type; 
          GHICHUTRAKETQUAfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.GHICHUTRAKETQUA%type;
          HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.HOSOTIEPNHANID%type;
          --LYDOXOATAMTHOIfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.LYDOXOATAMTHOI%type; 
          MOTATOMTATfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.MOTATOMTAT%type;
          NGAYHENLAYPHIEUCHUYENTHUEfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.NGAYHENLAYPHIEUCHUYENTHUE%type;
          NGAYHENTRAHOSOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.NGAYHENTRAHOSO%type;
          NGAYTIEPNHANHOSOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.NGAYTIEPNHANHOSO%type;
          NGAYTRAKETQUAfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.NGAYTRAKETQUA%type; 
          NGUOICAPNHATIDfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.NGUOICAPNHATID%type;
          NGUOINHANKQHSfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.NGUOINHANKQHS%type; 
          NGUOINOPHOSOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.NGUOINOPHOSO%type; 
          PHUONGPHAPNHANTHONGBAOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.PHUONGPHAPNHANTHONGBAO%type; 
          QUYENTIEPNHANfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.QUYENTIEPNHAN%type;
          SOBIENNHANfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.SOBIENNHAN%type; 
          SODIENTHOAIfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.SODIENTHOAI%type; 
          SOGIAYTOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.SOGIAYTO%type; 
          TENHOSOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.TENHOSO%type; 
          TENNGUOINHANKETQUAfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.TENNGUOINHANKETQUA%type;
          THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT%type;
          THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.THOIDIEMKHOITAO%type; 
          THUTUCHANHCHINHIDfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.THUTUCHANHCHINHID%type; 
          TINHTRANGHOSOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.TINHTRANGHOSO%type; 
          TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.TRANGTHAIHOSOID%type; 
          TUCACHNGUOINHANKETQUAfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.TUCACHNGUOINHANKETQUA%type; 
          TUCACHNGUOINOPHOSOfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.TUCACHNGUOINOPHOSO%type;
          UIDfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN."UID"%type;
          XULYTHEOQUYTRINHfld QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN.XULYTHEOQUYTRINH%type;  
          
        CURSOR hstn_cursor IS 
        SELECT HOSOTIEPNHANID ,
                THUTUCHANHCHINHID ,
                CAP ,
                DONVIHANHCHINHID ,
                SOBIENNHAN ,
                QUYENTIEPNHAN ,
                CANBOTIEPNHANID ,
                NGAYTIEPNHANHOSO ,
                NGAYHENTRAHOSO ,
                NGUOINOPHOSO ,
                TUCACHNGUOINOPHOSO ,
                MOTATOMTAT ,
                SODIENTHOAI ,
                EMAIL ,
                SOGIAYTO ,
                PHUONGPHAPNHANTHONGBAO ,
                DIACHINGUOINOPHS ,
                TENNGUOINHANKETQUA ,
                TUCACHNGUOINHANKETQUA ,
                DIACHINGUOINHANKETQUA ,
                NGUOINHANKQHS ,
                NGAYTRAKETQUA ,
                GHICHUTRAKETQUA ,
                TINHTRANGHOSO ,
                XULYTHEOQUYTRINH ,
                TRANGTHAIHOSOID ,
                "UID" ,
                THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
                NGUOICAPNHATID ,
                THOIDIEMCAPNHAT ,
                NGAYHENLAYPHIEUCHUYENTHUE ,
                TENHOSO  FROM "MPLIS"."QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN"
        WHERE hstn_id = "HOSOTIEPNHANID";
        
        --row_hstn hstn_cursor%ROWTYPE;
        
    BEGIN
      -- TODO: Implementation required for PROCEDURE HOSOTIEPNHAN.select_hstn            
      --hstnid := '557fa65f-2d59-4d04-b914-401fa7ba20c4';
      --sodoqt_id := e5af7f48-2ba4-42bb-81c6-08792f0707f6
      
      OPEN hstn_cursor;
      LOOP
        FETCH hstn_cursor INTO 
            HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
            THUTUCHANHCHINHIDfld ,
            CAPfld ,
            DONVIHANHCHINHIDfld ,
            SOBIENNHANfld ,
            QUYENTIEPNHANfld ,
            CANBOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
            NGAYTIEPNHANHOSOfld ,
            NGAYHENTRAHOSOfld ,
            NGUOINOPHOSOfld ,
            TUCACHNGUOINOPHOSOfld ,
            MOTATOMTATfld ,
            SODIENTHOAIfld ,
            EMAILfld ,
            SOGIAYTOfld ,
            PHUONGPHAPNHANTHONGBAOfld ,
            DIACHINGUOINOPHSfld ,
            TENNGUOINHANKETQUAfld ,
            TUCACHNGUOINHANKETQUAfld ,
            DIACHINGUOINHANKETQUAfld ,
            NGUOINHANKQHSfld ,
            NGAYTRAKETQUAfld ,
            GHICHUTRAKETQUAfld ,
            TINHTRANGHOSOfld ,
            XULYTHEOQUYTRINHfld ,
            TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld ,
            UIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld ,
            NGAYHENLAYPHIEUCHUYENTHUEfld ,
            TENHOSOfld;
          
        EXIT WHEN hstn_cursor%NOTFOUND;
      
        INSERT INTO QT_HOSOTIEPNHAN_XOATAMTHOI(
              HOSOTIEPNHANID ,
              THUTUCHANHCHINHID ,
              CAP ,
              DONVIHANHCHINHID ,
              SOBIENNHAN ,
              QUYENTIEPNHAN ,
              CANBOTIEPNHANID ,
              NGAYTIEPNHANHOSO ,
              NGAYHENTRAHOSO ,
              NGUOINOPHOSO ,
              TUCACHNGUOINOPHOSO ,
              MOTATOMTAT ,
              SODIENTHOAI ,
              EMAIL ,
              SOGIAYTO ,
              PHUONGPHAPNHANTHONGBAO ,
              DIACHINGUOINOPHS ,
              TENNGUOINHANKETQUA ,
              TUCACHNGUOINHANKETQUA ,
              DIACHINGUOINHANKETQUA ,
              NGUOINHANKQHS ,
              NGAYTRAKETQUA ,
              GHICHUTRAKETQUA ,
              TINHTRANGHOSO ,
              XULYTHEOQUYTRINH ,
              TRANGTHAIHOSOID ,
              LYDOXOATAMTHOI,
              "UID" ,
              THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
              NGUOICAPNHATID ,
              THOIDIEMCAPNHAT ,
              NGAYHENLAYPHIEUCHUYENTHUE ,
              TENHOSO
          )
          VALUES (
              HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
              THUTUCHANHCHINHIDfld ,
              CAPfld ,
              DONVIHANHCHINHIDfld ,
              SOBIENNHANfld ,
              QUYENTIEPNHANfld ,
              CANBOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
              NGAYTIEPNHANHOSOfld ,
              NGAYHENTRAHOSOfld ,
              NGUOINOPHOSOfld ,
              TUCACHNGUOINOPHOSOfld ,
              MOTATOMTATfld ,
              SODIENTHOAIfld ,
              EMAILfld ,
              SOGIAYTOfld ,
              PHUONGPHAPNHANTHONGBAOfld ,
              DIACHINGUOINOPHSfld ,
              TENNGUOINHANKETQUAfld ,
              TUCACHNGUOINHANKETQUAfld ,
              DIACHINGUOINHANKETQUAfld ,
              NGUOINHANKQHSfld ,
              NGAYTRAKETQUAfld ,
              GHICHUTRAKETQUAfld ,
              TINHTRANGHOSOfld ,
              XULYTHEOQUYTRINHfld ,
              TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld ,
              stlydoxoatamthoi,
              UIDfld ,
              THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
              NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
              THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld ,
              NGAYHENLAYPHIEUCHUYENTHUEfld ,
              TENHOSOfld
          );
                
      END LOOP;
      CLOSE hstn_cursor;     
      --NULL;
            LuuXuLyHoSo_TamThoi(hstn_id, sodoquytrinh_id);
            LuuFileDinhKemHoSo_TamThoi(hstn_id);
            --LuuTrangThaiHoSo_TamThoi(hstn_id, sodoquytrinh_id);
            --LuuFileDinhKemHoSo_TamThoi (hstn_id);
    END LuuHoSoTiepNhan_TamThoi;

    --------------------------------------------------------|
    -- Hàm b¿n ghi b¿ xóa ¿ b¿ng XULYHOSO vào b¿ng t¿m --|
    --------------------------------------------------------|
    PROCEDURE LuuXuLyHoSo_TamThoi(hstn_id IN STRING, sodoqt_id IN STRING) AS
      
            XULYHOSOIDfld QT_XULYHOSO.XULYHOSOID%type;
            HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld QT_XULYHOSO.HOSOTIEPNHANID%type;
            SODOQUYTRINHIDfld QT_XULYHOSO.SODOQUYTRINHID%type;
            LOAITIEPNHANfld QT_XULYHOSO.LOAITIEPNHAN%type;
            THUTUTHUCHIENfld QT_XULYHOSO.THUTUTHUCHIEN%type;
            DANGTHUCHIENfld QT_XULYHOSO.DANGTHUCHIEN%type;
            BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld QT_XULYHOSO.BUOCQUYTRINHID%type;
            BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCIDfld QT_XULYHOSO.BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCID%type;
            NGAYBATDAUXULYfld QT_XULYHOSO.NGAYBATDAUXULY%type;
            NGAYDUKIENTRAKETQUAfld QT_XULYHOSO.NGAYDUKIENTRAKETQUA%type;
            NGAYTRAKETQUAfld QT_XULYHOSO.NGAYTRAKETQUA%type;
            UIDfld QT_XULYHOSO."UID"%type;
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld QT_XULYHOSO.THOIDIEMKHOITAO%type;
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld QT_XULYHOSO.NGUOICAPNHATID%type;
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld QT_XULYHOSO.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT%type;
      
      CURSOR xulyhs_cursor IS 
        SELECT 
            XULYHOSOID ,
            HOSOTIEPNHANID ,
            SODOQUYTRINHID ,
            LOAITIEPNHAN ,
            THUTUTHUCHIEN ,
            DANGTHUCHIEN ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHID ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCID ,
            NGAYBATDAUXULY ,
            NGAYDUKIENTRAKETQUA ,
            NGAYTRAKETQUA ,
            "UID" ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
            NGUOICAPNHATID ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHAT 
        FROM "MPLIS"."QT_XULYHOSO"
        WHERE hstn_id = "HOSOTIEPNHANID" AND sodoqt_id = "SODOQUYTRINHID";
        
      BEGIN
      
        OPEN xulyhs_cursor;
        LOOP
          FETCH xulyhs_cursor INTO 
            XULYHOSOIDfld ,
            HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
            SODOQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            LOAITIEPNHANfld ,
            THUTUTHUCHIENfld ,
            DANGTHUCHIENfld ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCIDfld ,
            NGAYBATDAUXULYfld ,
            NGAYDUKIENTRAKETQUAfld ,
            NGAYTRAKETQUAfld ,
            UIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld;
              
          EXIT WHEN xulyhs_cursor%NOTFOUND;
        
          INSERT INTO QT_XULYHOSO_XOATAMTHOI(
                XULYHOSOID ,
                HOSOTIEPNHANID ,
                SODOQUYTRINHID ,
                LOAITIEPNHAN ,
                THUTUTHUCHIEN ,
                DANGTHUCHIEN ,
                BUOCQUYTRINHID ,
                BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCID ,
                NGAYBATDAUXULY ,
                NGAYDUKIENTRAKETQUA ,
                NGAYTRAKETQUA ,
                "UID" ,
                THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
                NGUOICAPNHATID ,
                THOIDIEMCAPNHAT 
            )
            VALUES (
                XULYHOSOIDfld ,
                HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
                SODOQUYTRINHIDfld ,
                LOAITIEPNHANfld ,
                THUTUTHUCHIENfld ,
                DANGTHUCHIENfld ,
                BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld ,
                BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCIDfld ,
                NGAYBATDAUXULYfld ,
                NGAYDUKIENTRAKETQUAfld ,
                NGAYTRAKETQUAfld ,
                UIDfld ,
                THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
                NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
                THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld
            );
                  
        END LOOP;
        CLOSE xulyhs_cursor;
        
        --NULL;
        LuuTrangThaiHoSo_TamThoi(hstn_id, sodoqt_id, XULYHOSOIDfld);
    END LuuXuLyHoSo_TamThoi;

  
    ----------------------------------------------------------|
    -- Hàm b¿n ghi b¿ xóa ¿ b¿ng TRANGTHAIHOSO vào b¿ng t¿m --|
    ----------------------------------------------------------|
    PROCEDURE LuuTrangThaiHoSo_TamThoi (hstiepnhan_id IN STRING, sodoqt_id IN STRING, xulyhs_id IN STRING) AS
      
            TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld  QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.TRANGTHAIHOSOID%type;
            XULYHOSOIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.XULYHOSOID%type;
            SODOQUYTRINHIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.SODOQUYTRINHID%type;
            BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.BUOCQUYTRINHID%type;
            HANHDONGIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.HANHDONGID%type;
            CHUCNANGIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.CHUCNANGID%type;
            NGUOIXULYIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.NGUOIXULYID%type;
            NGAYHOSODENfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.NGAYHOSODEN%type;
            NGAYHOANTHANHfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.NGAYHOANTHANH%type;
            TINHTRANGXULYfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.TINHTRANGXULY%type;
            YKIENfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.YKIEN%type;
            GIATRIBIENDAUVAOfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.GIATRIBIENDAUVAO%type;
            GIATRIBIENDAURAfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.GIATRIBIENDAURA%type;
            THUCHIENLAIfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.THUCHIENLAI%type;
            UIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO."UID"%type;
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.THOIDIEMKHOITAO%type;
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.NGUOICAPNHATID%type;
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT%type;
            BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCIDfld QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO.BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCID%type;
           
      
      CURSOR trangthaihs_cursor IS 
        SELECT 
            TRANGTHAIHOSOID ,
            XULYHOSOID ,
            SODOQUYTRINHID ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHID ,
            HANHDONGID ,
            CHUCNANGID ,
            NGUOIXULYID ,
            NGAYHOSODEN ,
            NGAYHOANTHANH ,
            TINHTRANGXULY ,
            YKIEN ,
            GIATRIBIENDAUVAO ,
            GIATRIBIENDAURA ,
            THUCHIENLAI ,
            "UID" ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
            NGUOICAPNHATID ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHAT ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCID 
        FROM "MPLIS"."QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO"
        WHERE xulyhs_id = "XULYHOSOID" AND sodoqt_id = "SODOQUYTRINHID";
        
      BEGIN
      
        OPEN trangthaihs_cursor;
        LOOP
          FETCH trangthaihs_cursor INTO 
            TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld ,
            XULYHOSOIDfld ,
            SODOQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            HANHDONGIDfld ,
            CHUCNANGIDfld ,
            NGUOIXULYIDfld ,
            NGAYHOSODENfld ,
            NGAYHOANTHANHfld ,
            TINHTRANGXULYfld ,
            YKIENfld ,
            GIATRIBIENDAUVAOfld ,
            GIATRIBIENDAURAfld ,
            THUCHIENLAIfld ,
            UIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCIDfld;
              
          EXIT WHEN trangthaihs_cursor%NOTFOUND;
        
          INSERT INTO QT_TRANGTHAIHOSO_XOATAMTHOI(
                TRANGTHAIHOSOID ,
                XULYHOSOID ,
                SODOQUYTRINHID ,
                BUOCQUYTRINHID ,
                HANHDONGID ,
                CHUCNANGID ,
                NGUOIXULYID ,
                NGAYHOSODEN ,
                NGAYHOANTHANH ,
                TINHTRANGXULY ,
                YKIEN ,
                GIATRIBIENDAUVAO ,
                GIATRIBIENDAURA ,
                THUCHIENLAI ,
                "UID" ,
                THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
                NGUOICAPNHATID ,
                THOIDIEMCAPNHAT ,                
                BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCID  
            )
            VALUES (
                TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld ,
                XULYHOSOIDfld ,
                SODOQUYTRINHIDfld ,
                BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld ,
                HANHDONGIDfld ,
                CHUCNANGIDfld ,
                NGUOIXULYIDfld ,
                NGAYHOSODENfld ,
                NGAYHOANTHANHfld ,
                TINHTRANGXULYfld ,
                YKIENfld ,
                GIATRIBIENDAUVAOfld ,
                GIATRIBIENDAURAfld ,
                THUCHIENLAIfld ,
                UIDfld ,
                THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
                NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
                THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld ,                
                BUOCQUYTRINHTRUOCIDfld
            );
                  
        END LOOP;
        CLOSE trangthaihs_cursor;
        
        NULL;
    END LuuTrangThaiHoSo_TamThoi;
    
    -----------------------------------------------------------------------|
    -- Hàm b¿n ghi b¿ xóa ¿ b¿ng FILEDINHKEMHOSO_XOATAMTHOI vào b¿ng t¿m --|
    -----------------------------------------------------------------------|
    PROCEDURE LuuFileDinhKemHoSo_TamThoi (hstiepnhan_id IN STRING) AS
      
            FILEDINHKEMHOSOIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.FILEDINHKEMHOSOID%type;
            HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.HOSOTIEPNHANID%type;
            TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.TRANGTHAIHOSOID%type;
            LOAIGIAYTOKEMTHEOHOSOIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.LOAIGIAYTOKEMTHEOHOSOID%type;
            SODOQUYTRINHIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.SODOQUYTRINHID%type;
            BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.BUOCQUYTRINHID%type;
            TENFILEfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.TENFILE%type;
            NGAYTAOFILEfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.NGAYTAOFILE%type;
            NGUOITAOFILEIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.NGUOITAOFILEID%type;
            LOAIfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.LOAI%type;
            SOLUONGfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.SOLUONG%type;
            GHICHUfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.GHICHU%type;
            DUONGDANFILEfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.DUONGDANFILE%type;
            UIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO."UID"%type;
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.THOIDIEMKHOITAO%type;
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.NGUOICAPNHATID%type;
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT%type;
            LOAIBAOCAOfld QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO.LOAIBAOCAO%type;
      
      CURSOR filedinhkemhs_cursor IS 
        SELECT 
            FILEDINHKEMHOSOID ,
            HOSOTIEPNHANID ,
            TRANGTHAIHOSOID ,
            LOAIGIAYTOKEMTHEOHOSOID ,
            SODOQUYTRINHID ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHID ,
            TENFILE ,
            NGAYTAOFILE ,
            NGUOITAOFILEID ,
            LOAI ,
            SOLUONG ,
            GHICHU ,
            DUONGDANFILE ,
            "UID" ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
            NGUOICAPNHATID ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHAT ,
            LOAIBAOCAO  
        FROM "MPLIS"."QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO"
        WHERE hstiepnhan_id = "HOSOTIEPNHANID";
        
      BEGIN
      
        OPEN filedinhkemhs_cursor;
        LOOP
          FETCH filedinhkemhs_cursor INTO 
            FILEDINHKEMHOSOIDfld ,
            HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
            TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld ,
            LOAIGIAYTOKEMTHEOHOSOIDfld ,
            SODOQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            TENFILEfld ,
            NGAYTAOFILEfld ,
            NGUOITAOFILEIDfld ,
            LOAIfld ,
            SOLUONGfld ,
            GHICHUfld ,
            DUONGDANFILEfld ,
            UIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld ,
            LOAIBAOCAOfld;
              
          EXIT WHEN filedinhkemhs_cursor%NOTFOUND;
        
          INSERT INTO QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO_XOATAMTHOI(
                FILEDINHKEMHOSOID ,
                HOSOTIEPNHANID ,
                TRANGTHAIHOSOID ,
                LOAIGIAYTOKEMTHEOHOSOID ,
                SODOQUYTRINHID ,
                BUOCQUYTRINHID ,
                TENFILE ,
                NGAYTAOFILE ,
                NGUOITAOFILEID ,
                LOAI ,
                SOLUONG ,
                GHICHU ,
                DUONGDANFILE ,
                "UID" ,
                THOIDIEMKHOITAO ,
                NGUOICAPNHATID ,
                THOIDIEMCAPNHAT ,
                LOAIBAOCAO  
            )
            VALUES (
                FILEDINHKEMHOSOIDfld ,
            HOSOTIEPNHANIDfld ,
            TRANGTHAIHOSOIDfld ,
            LOAIGIAYTOKEMTHEOHOSOIDfld ,
            SODOQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            BUOCQUYTRINHIDfld ,
            TENFILEfld ,
            NGAYTAOFILEfld ,
            NGUOITAOFILEIDfld ,
            LOAIfld ,
            SOLUONGfld ,
            GHICHUfld ,
            DUONGDANFILEfld ,
            UIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMKHOITAOfld ,
            NGUOICAPNHATIDfld ,
            THOIDIEMCAPNHATfld ,
            LOAIBAOCAOfld
            );
                  
        END LOOP;
        CLOSE filedinhkemhs_cursor;
        
        NULL;
    END LuuFileDinhKemHoSo_TamThoi;
    
END QUYTRINH_HOSO;

--
-- LCHSV_TAILIEUDODAC_LOAIBDDC  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.LCHSV_TAILIEUDODAC_LOAIBDDC
(TAILIEUDODACID, XAID, TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH, TENTAILIEU, DONVIDODAC, 
 PHUONGPHAPDO, MUCDOCHINHXAC, TYLEDODAC, NGAYHOANTHANH)
AS 
SELECT TL.TAILIEUDODACID,TL.XAID
,L.TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH , TL.TENTAILIEU, TL.DONVIDODAC,TL.PHUONGPHAPDO,TL.MUCDOCHINHXAC,TL.TYLEDODAC,TL.NGAYHOANTHANH

FROM DC_TAILIEUDODAC TL
LEFT JOIN DM_LOAIBANDODIACHINH L ON TL.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID = L.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID;


--
-- VIEW_TLDD_BDDC_XA  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_TLDD_BDDC_XA
(TAILIEUDODACID, XAID, LOAIBANDODIACHINHID, DONVIDODAC, PHUONGPHAPDO, 
 MUCDOCHINHXAC, TYLEDODAC, NGAYHOANTHANH, TENTAILIEU, GHICHU, 
 MALOAIBANDODIACHINH, TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH, MAXA, TENXA)
AS 
SELECT T.TAILIEUDODACID,T.XAID,T.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID,T.DONVIDODAC,T.PHUONGPHAPDO
,T.MUCDOCHINHXAC,T.TYLEDODAC,T.NGAYHOANTHANH,T.TENTAILIEU,T.GHICHU
,D.MALOAIBANDODIACHINH,D.TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH
,X.MAXA,X.TENXA
FROM DC_TAILIEUDODAC T
LEFT JOIN DM_LOAIBANDODIACHINH D on D.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID = T.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID
LEFT JOIN HC_XA  X ON X.XAID = T.XAID;


--
-- VIEW_THUA  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_THUA
(THUADATID, SOHIEUTOBANDO, SOTHUTUTHUA, DIENTICH, DIENTICHPHAPLY, 
 MAXA, DIACHI, NGAYHOANTHANH, TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH, TAILIEUDODACID, 
 LOAIBANDODIACHINHID)
AS 
SELECT   T.THUADATID,t.SOHIEUTOBANDO, T.SOTHUTUTHUA,T.DIENTICH,
 	T.DIENTICHPHAPLY,T. MAXA, T.DIACHI,TL.NGAYHOANTHANH, DMBD.TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH, TL.TAILIEUDODACID,DMBD.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID
				FROM DC_THUADAT T 
                LEFT JOIN  DC_TAILIEUDODAC TL ON T.TAILIEUDODACID = TL.TAILIEUDODACID
                LEFT JOIN DM_LOAIBANDODIACHINH DMBD ON DMBD.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID = TL.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID
ORDER BY T.THUADATID;


--
-- HSV_LICHSU  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HSV_LICHSU
(LICHSUHOSOID, HOSOTRUOCID, HOSOID, HOSOSAUID, XAID, 
 TENXA, TENHOSOHIENTAI, TENHOSOTRUOC, TENHOSOSAU)
AS 
SELECT  HS_LICHSU.LICHSUHOSOID, HS_LICHSU.HOSOTRUOCID
,HS_LICHSU.HOSOID, HS_LICHSU.HOSOSAUID, HS_LICHSU.XAID , HC_XA.TENXA
,(SELECT TENHOSO FROM HS_HOSO WHERE HS_HOSO.HOSOID = HS_LICHSU.HOSOID) TENHOSOHIENTAI

,(SELECT TENHOSO FROM HS_HOSO WHERE HS_HOSO.HOSOID = HS_LICHSU.HOSOTRUOCID) TENHOSOTRUOC

, (SELECT TENHOSO FROM HS_HOSO WHERE HS_HOSO.HOSOID = HS_LICHSU.HOSOSAUID) TENHOSOSAU


FROM HS_LICHSU LEFT JOIN HC_XA ON HS_LICHSU.XAID = HC_XA.XAID;


--
-- VIEW_DONDK  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_DONDK
(DONDANGKYID, NGAYDANGKY, HOSOTIEPNHANID, NGUOIID_QQL, THUADAT_QQL, 
 DAMUCDICHSUDUNGID_QQL, NGUOIID_QSH, TAISANGANLIENVOIDATID, GIAYCHUNGNHANID_QSH, NGUOIID_QSD, 
 THUADATID_QSD, MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID_QSD, GIAYCHUNGNHANID_QSD)
AS 
select D.DONDANGKYID,d.NGAYDANGKY,d.HOSOTIEPNHANID,
 QQL.NGUOIID as NGUOIID_QQL,
  QQL.THUADATID as THUADAT_QQL,
  QQL.DAMUCDICHSUDUNGID as DAMUCDICHSUDUNGID_QQl,
  QSH.NGUOIID as NGUOIID_QSH,
  QSH.TAISANGANLIENVOIDATID,
  QSH.GIAYCHUNGNHANID GIAYCHUNGNHANID_QSH,
  QSD.NGUOIID as NGUOIID_QSD ,
  QSD.THUADATID as THUADATID_QSD,
  QSD.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID as MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID_QSD,
  QSD.GIAYCHUNGNHANID as GIAYCHUNGNHANID_QSD
				From DC_DONDANGKY D
                left join DC_QUYENQUANLYDAT QQL on QQL.DONDANGKYID = D.DONDANGKYID
                left join DC_QUYENSOHUUTAISAN QSH on QSH.DONDANGKYID = D.DONDANGKYID
                left join DC_QUYENSUDUNGDAT QSD on QSD.DONDANGKYID = D.DONDANGKYID
 order by D.DONDANGKYID;


--
-- VIEW_THUADAT_VOCHONG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_THUADAT_VOCHONG
(HOTEN, DIACHIDAYDU, GIOITINH, CANHANID, SOGIAYTO, 
 CHONG, VO, NGUOIID, THUADATID, MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID, 
 DONDANGKYID, QUYENSUDUNGDATID)
AS 
select ttvc.HOTEN,ttvc.DIACHIDAYDU,ttvc.GIOITINH, ttvc.CANHANID, ttvc.SOGIAYTO,ttvc.CHONG, ttvc.VO,
C.NGUOIID,
  C.THUADATID ,C.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID, C.DONDANGKYID, C.QUYENSUDUNGDATID
from
(select  A.HOTEN,A.DIACHIDAYDU,A.GIOITINH, A.CANHANID, A.SOGIAYTO,B.NGUOIID,B.CHONG, B.VO
from
(SELECT  CN.HOTEN,CN.DIACHIDAYDU,CN.GIOITINH, CN.CANHANID, GT.SOGIAYTO
				FROM DC_CANHAN CN
                INNER JOIN  DC_GIAYTOTUYTHAN GT ON GT.CANHANID = CN.CANHANID

                ) A
		INNER JOIN
(SELECT N.NGUOIID,VC.CHONG, VC.VO,
  N.LOAIDOITUONGID
				FROM DC_NGUOI N
                INNER JOIN  DC_VOCHONG VC ON VC.VOCHONGID =N.CHITIETID
                where N.LOAIDOITUONGID =2
               ) B
on A.CANHANID =B.Vo or A.CANHANID =B.Chong
order by b.nguoiid) ttvc
inner join
(SELECT N.NGUOIID,
  QSD.THUADATID ,QSD.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID, QSD.DONDANGKYID, QSD.QUYENSUDUNGDATID
				FROM DC_NGUOI N
                INNER JOIN  DC_QUYENSUDUNGDAT QSD ON QSD.NGUOIID = N.NGUOIID
                where N.LOAIDOITUONGID =2
               ) C
  on ttvc.NguoiID =c.NguoiID
  order by C.DONDANGKYID;


--
-- VIEW_THUA_CANHAN  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_THUA_CANHAN
(HOTEN, DIACHIDAYDU, GIOITINH, CANHANID, SOGIAYTO, 
 NGUOIID, CHITIETID, LOAIDOITUONGID, THUADATID, MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID, 
 DONDANGKYID, QUYENSUDUNGDATID)
AS 
SELECT "HOTEN","DIACHIDAYDU","GIOITINH","CANHANID","SOGIAYTO","NGUOIID","CHITIETID","LOAIDOITUONGID","THUADATID","MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID","DONDANGKYID","QUYENSUDUNGDATID"
FROM
(SELECT  CN.HOTEN,CN.DIACHIDAYDU,CN.GIOITINH, CN.CANHANID, GT.SOGIAYTO
				FROM DC_CANHAN CN
                INNER JOIN  DC_GIAYTOTUYTHAN GT ON GT.CANHANID = CN.CANHANID

                ) A
		INNER JOIN
(SELECT N.NGUOIID,N.CHITIETID,
  N.LOAIDOITUONGID,QSD.THUADATID ,QSD.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID, QSD.DONDANGKYID, QSD.QUYENSUDUNGDATID
				FROM DC_NGUOI N
                INNER JOIN  DC_QUYENSUDUNGDAT QSD ON QSD.NGUOIID = N.NGUOIID
                where N.LOAIDOITUONGID =1
               ) B
ON A.CANHANID = B.CHITIETID
ORDER BY B.THUADATID ,B.DONDANGKYID,B.QUYENSUDUNGDATID;


--
-- VIEW_THUADAT  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.VIEW_THUADAT
(THUADATID, SOHIEUTOBANDO, SOTHUTUTHUA, DIENTICH, DIENTICHPHAPLY, 
 MAXA, DIACHI, SUDUNGCHUNG, THOIHANSUDUNG, LAMUCDICHCHINH, 
 TENMUCDICHSUDUNG, MAMUCDICHSUDUNG, MANGUONGOCSUDUNG, TENNGUONGOCSUDUNG, NGAYHOANTHANH, 
 TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH, TAILIEUDODACID, LOAIBANDODIACHINHID, MUCDICHSUDUNGID, LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID, 
 MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID)
AS 
SELECT A.THUADATID,A.SOHIEUTOBANDO, A.SOTHUTUTHUA,A.DIENTICH,
 	A.DIENTICHPHAPLY,A. MAXA, A.DIACHI, A.SUDUNGCHUNG,A.THOIHANSUDUNG, 
 	A.LAMUCDICHCHINH,A.TENMUCDICHSUDUNG,
	A.MAMUCDICHSUDUNG, A.MANGUONGOCSUDUNG,A.TENNGUONGOCSUDUNG,
	B.NGAYHOANTHANH, B.TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH,
	B.TAILIEUDODACID,B.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID,A.MUCDICHSUDUNGID,A.LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID, A.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID
FROM
(SELECT  T.THUADATID,T.SOHIEUTOBANDO, T.SOTHUTUTHUA,T.DIENTICH,
  T.DIENTICHPHAPLY, T. MAXA, 
  T.DIACHI, M.SUDUNGCHUNG,
  M.THOIHANSUDUNG,
  M.LAMUCDICHCHINH,DM.TENMUCDICHSUDUNG, DM.MAMUCDICHSUDUNG,DMNG.MANGUONGOCSUDUNG,DMNG.TENNGUONGOCSUDUNG,
 	M.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID ,DM.MUCDICHSUDUNGID,DMNG.LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID
				FROM DC_THUADAT T 
                LEFT JOIN  DC_MUCDICHSUDUNGDAT M ON T.THUADATID = M.THUADATID
                LEFT JOIN DM_MUCDICHSUDUNG DM ON DM.MUCDICHSUDUNGID =M.MUCDICHSUDUNGID
                LEFT JOIN DC_NGUONGOCSUDUNG NG ON M.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID = NG.MUCDICHSUDUNGDATID 
                 LEFT JOIN DM_LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNG DMNG ON DMNG.LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID = NG.LOAINGUONGOCSUDUNGID ) A
		LEFT JOIN
(SELECT   T.THUADATID,TL.NGAYHOANTHANH, DMBD.TENLOAIBANDODIACHINH, TL.TAILIEUDODACID,DMBD.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID
				FROM DC_THUADAT T 
                LEFT JOIN  DC_TAILIEUDODAC TL ON T.TAILIEUDODACID = TL.TAILIEUDODACID
                LEFT JOIN DM_LOAIBANDODIACHINH DMBD ON DMBD.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID = TL.LOAIBANDODIACHINHID) B
ON A.THUADATID= B.THUADATID
ORDER BY A.THUADATID;


--
-- HTV_NGUOIDUNG_CHUCNANG  (View) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW MPLIS.HTV_NGUOIDUNG_CHUCNANG
(NGUOIDUNGID, MACHUCNANG, CHOPHEPSUDUNG)
AS 
SELECT HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID, HT_CHUCNANG.MACHUCNANG, HT_CHUCNANG.CHOPHEPSUDUNG
    
FROM HT_NGUOIDUNG INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG ON HT_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID = HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG.NGUOIDUNGID  INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC ON HT_TOCHUC_NGUOIDUNG.TOCHUCID = HT_TOCHUC.TOCHUCID INNER JOIN HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG ON HT_TOCHUC.TOCHUCID = HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG.TOCHUCID INNER JOIN HT_NHOMCHUCNANG ON HT_TOCHUC_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID = HT_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID INNER JOIN HT_CHUCNANG_NHOMCHUCNANG ON HT_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID = HT_CHUCNANG_NHOMCHUCNANG.NHOMCHUCNANGID INNER JOIN HT_CHUCNANG ON HT_CHUCNANG_NHOMCHUCNANG.CHUCNANGID = HT_CHUCNANG.CHUCNANGID;


--
-- QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO_IN_UP  (Trigger) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER MPLIS.QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO_IN_UP
  before update or insert  ON MPLIS.QT_FILEDINHKEMHOSO  
  for each row
declare
  v_date date := sysdate;
begin
  --neu la insert 
  if inserting then
    :new.THOIDIEMKHOITAO := v_date;
    :new.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT := v_date;
  end if;
  --neu la update
  if updating then
    :new.THOIDIEMCAPNHAT := v_date;
  end if;

end;
/

--
-- DC_QUYENSUDUNGDAT_QUYENSUDUNGD  (Trigger) 
--
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER MPLIS.DC_QUYENSUDUNGDAT_QUYENSUDUNGD BEFORE
  INSERT ON MPLIS.DC_QUYENSUDUNGDAT FOR EACH ROW
WHEN (
NEW.quyenSuDungDatId IS NULL
      )
BEGIN :NEW.quyenSuDungDatId := DC_QuyenSuDungDat_quyenSuDungD.NEXTVAL;
END;
/


--
-- DBA  (Role) 
--
CREATE ROLE DBA NOT IDENTIFIED;

GRANT CREATE SESSION TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER SESSION TO DBA;
GRANT DROP TABLESPACE TO DBA;
GRANT BECOME USER TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ROLLBACK SEGMENT TO DBA;
GRANT SELECT ANY TABLE TO DBA;
GRANT INSERT ANY TABLE TO DBA;
GRANT UPDATE ANY TABLE TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY INDEX TO DBA;
GRANT SELECT ANY SEQUENCE TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE ROLE TO DBA;
GRANT EXECUTE ANY PROCEDURE TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER PROFILE TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE ANY DIRECTORY TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE ANY LIBRARY TO DBA;
GRANT EXECUTE ANY LIBRARY TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY INDEXTYPE TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY INDEXTYPE TO DBA;
BEGIN
SYS.DBMS_AQADM.GRANT_SYSTEM_PRIVILEGE (
  PRIVILEGE    => 'DEQUEUE_ANY',
  GRANTEE      => 'DBA',
  ADMIN_OPTION => FALSE);
END;
/
BEGIN
SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.GRANT_SYSTEM_PRIVILEGE(
  PRIVILEGE    => SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.EXECUTE_ANY_EVALUATION_CONTEXT,
  GRANTEE      => 'DBA',
  GRANT_OPTION => FALSE);
END;
/
GRANT EXPORT FULL DATABASE TO DBA;
BEGIN
SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.GRANT_SYSTEM_PRIVILEGE(
  PRIVILEGE    => SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.CREATE_RULE_OBJ,
  GRANTEE      => 'DBA',
  GRANT_OPTION => FALSE);
END;
/
GRANT ALTER ANY SQL PROFILE TO DBA;
GRANT ADMINISTER ANY SQL TUNING SET TO DBA;
GRANT CHANGE NOTIFICATION TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY EDITION TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY MINING MODEL TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY MINING MODEL TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY CUBE DIMENSION TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE CUBE TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY CUBE BUILD PROCESS TO DBA;
GRANT USE ANY SQL TRANSLATION PROFILE TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE PLUGGABLE DATABASE TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ROLLBACK SEGMENT TO DBA;
GRANT DELETE ANY TABLE TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER DATABASE TO DBA;
GRANT FORCE ANY TRANSACTION TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY PROCEDURE TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY TRIGGER TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY MATERIALIZED VIEW TO DBA;
GRANT UNDER ANY TYPE TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY LIBRARY TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE DIMENSION TO DBA;
GRANT DEBUG ANY PROCEDURE TO DBA;
BEGIN
SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.GRANT_SYSTEM_PRIVILEGE(
  PRIVILEGE    => SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.CREATE_RULE_SET_OBJ,
  GRANTEE      => 'DBA',
  GRANT_OPTION => FALSE);
END;
/
BEGIN
SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.GRANT_SYSTEM_PRIVILEGE(
  PRIVILEGE    => SYS.DBMS_RULE_ADM.ALTER_ANY_RULE_SET,
  GRANTEE      => 'DBA',
  GRANT_OPTION => FALSE);
END;
/
GRANT ANALYZE ANY DICTIONARY TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY EDITION TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE ANY ASSEMBLY TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY CUBE TO DBA;
GRANT SELECT ANY CUBE TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY MEASURE FOLDER TO DBA;
GRANT RESTRICTED SESSION TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE TABLESPACE TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER TABLESPACE TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE USER TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER USER TO DBA;
GRANT LOCK ANY TABLE TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE VIEW TO DBA;
GRANT DROP ANY VIEW TO DBA;
GRANT GRANT ANY ROLE TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE TRIGGER TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE TYPE TO DBA;
GRANT EXECUTE ANY OPERATOR TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE ANY DIMENSION TO DBA;
GRANT ALTER ANY DIMENSION TO DBA;
GRANT CREATE ANY OUTLINE TO DBA;
GRANT ADMINISTER DATABASE TRIGGER TO DBA;
GRANT RESUMABLE TO DBA;
GRANT FLASHBACK ANY TABLE TO DBA;

--
-- DC_BD_GCN  (Table) 
--
CREATE TABLE MPLIS.DC_BD_GCN
(
  BDGCNID          VARCHAR2(36 BYTE) CONSTRAINT NN_DC_BD_GCN_BDGCNID NOT NULL,
  GIAYCHUNGNHANID  VARCHAR2(36 BYTE),
  BIENDONGID       VARCHAR2(36 BYTE),
  LAGCNVAO         CHAR(1 BYTE)
)
TABLESPACE MPLIS
RESULT_CACHE (MODE DEFAULT)
PCTUSED    0
PCTFREE    10
INITRANS   1
MAXTRANS   255
STORAGE    (
            INITIAL          128K
            NEXT             1M
            MINEXTENTS       1
            MAXEXTENTS       UNLIMITED
            PCTINCREASE      0
            BUFFER_POOL      DEFAULT
            FLASH_CACHE      DEFAULT
            CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT
           )
NOCOMPRESS ;
